  // Method to parse cookie value and set to window property
  // params:
  // cookieName: name of cookie to parse (string)
  // nullReturnValue: what to set if cookie doesn't exist (any)
  function getCookie(cookieName, nullReturnValue) {
     return document.cookie.split('; ').filter(
         function(pair){
             return pair.indexOf(cookieName + '=') == 0 })[0] ?
          document.cookie.split('; ').filter(
              function(pair){
                  return pair.indexOf(cookieName + '=') == 0 })[0].split('=')[1]
          : nullReturnValue;
  }

  /**
   * Utils function to inject script src tag
   */
  function injectScript(src, supportsCors, onload) {
    var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0],
        script = document.createElement('script');

    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    script.src = src;
    script.onload = onload || function() {};

    if (supportsCors) {
      script.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
    }

    head.appendChild(script);
  }

      s.crossOrigin = "anonymous";

<script>
   /*
   * Fire events after page load since Safari Performance Event entries are mutable
   * and loadEventEnd value is 0 till end of page load
  */ 
  addEventListener("load", () => { 
    const observer = new PerformanceObserver((list) => {
      list.getEntries().forEach((entry) => {
        if(entry.entryType === 'navigation') {
          const loadEventTime = entry.loadEventEnd - entry.startTime;
          if (loadEventTime > 0) {
            window.gtag('event', 'performance', {
              'metric_name': 'Page Load Time',
              'metric_value': loadEventTime,
              'load_tracking_type': 'Initial Load'
            })
          } else if (typeof(loadEventTime) !== 'number') {
            window?.dd?.warn('GA4 performance event payload not a number', {
              'metric_name': 'Page Load Time',
              'metric_value': loadEventTime,
              'load_tracking_type': 'Initial Load'
            })
          }
        }
      });
    });

    observer.observe({ entryTypes: ["navigation", "mark"] });
  
  });
</script>

.flex-straight[data-v-7b98bb81]{display:flex;align-items:flex-start;justify-content:center}.show-social-tablet[data-v-7b98bb81]{display:none}@media(max-width: 1350px){.show-social-tablet[data-v-7b98bb81]{margin-left:12px;display:block}}@media only screen and (min-width: 992px)and (max-width: 1750px){div.footer-desktop-left-nav__inner[data-v-7b98bb81]{margin-bottom:10px}}div.footer-desktop-left-nav__inner[data-v-7b98bb81]{display:flex}</style></head><body><script type="text/javascript">

  /* We do not support all browsers; When a user is using one of these
  unsupported browsers show them a warning. */

  (function() {

    /* Browsers with HTMLPictureElement defined should be modern enough to
    support everything we do [1]. Exceptions are IE 10-12 and Safari 8 which
    we support via an HTMLPictureElement polyfill, but adds support for many
    browsers including those we do not want to support (ie9, Safari7, ...).
    Thus we must find another way to not-warn said exceptions. We do this by
    UA sniffing (gasp)[2].

    [1] http://caniuse.com/#feat=picture
    [2] For details on our regex see http://regexr.com/3emos. */

    var polyfilledUserAgents = /MSIE 10|MSIE 11|IE 11|Trident.*rv:11|WOW64;.*rv:11|Edge\/12|AppleWebKit.*Version\/(:?8|9\.0|9\.1|9\.2)/;

    var isSupported = window.HTMLPictureElement
                   || polyfilledUserAgents.test(navigator.userAgent);

    if (!isSupported) {
      var div = document.createElement("div");
      div.innerHTML = "Sorry, your browser is not supported. You may experience some difficulties when shopping on SSENSE.";
      div.className = "message-box failed";
      div.style.position = "relative"; // [1]
      div.style.opacity = "1"; // [2]
      div.onclick = function () { document.body.removeChild(div); };
      document.body.insertBefore(div, document.body.firstChild); // [3]

      /*
      [1] .message-box is `position: fixed` so it "hovers" over body content,
      but we want this warning to push body content down instead.

      [2] .message-box is designed to be faded in by our JS app, but we cannot
      rely on any external JS here, so force opacity to 100%.

      [3] If firstChild is `null` then `insertBefore` will put `div` at
      end of child list of body which in this case would just mean first
      child. Reference:
      https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Node/insertBefore. */
    }
  })();
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">

  /* Include babel-polyfill if browser dos not support Object.assign or window.Promise */

  (function() {
    if (typeof Object.assign !== "function" ||
        typeof window.Promise !== "function") {

      var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0],
          script = document.createElement('script');

      script.type = 'text/javascript';
      script.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/babel-polyfill/7.8.7/polyfill.min.js';
      script.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
      head.appendChild(script);
    }
  })();
</script>

href="/en-us/women/designers/zimmermann" data-test="plpZimmermannLink"><span class="s-text">ZIMMERMANN</span></a></li></ul></nav></div></div> <div class="s-column plp-products-column__wrapper" style="width:calc(100% / 0.125);"><div><div class="s-row" style="margin-bottom:25px;"><div class="plp-description__wrapper"><div class="s-row" style="margin-bottom:0px;"><h1 class="plp-description__brand-title s-text s-text--uppercase s-text--font-weight-bold s-text--font-family-regular">
adidas Originals
</h1></div> <div class="s-row" style="margin-bottom:0px;"><div>
Introduced in 2001, adidas Originals is the heritage and lifestyle reserve of the legendary activewear label adidas. Adopting the iconic trefoil logo—the trifurcated symbol that first appeared in 1972—the offshoot brand issues a revival of vintage adidas wardrobe essentials, serving them up for the contemporary moment. The dynamic line is home to adidas’s ever-expanding roster of collaborations with designers, artists, and celebrities, hatching special editions of legendary styles like the Stan Smith sneaker or the Firebird tracksuit. Carrying forward the rich history of a veritable cultural icon, adidas Originals proves that a classic never goes out of style.
